./Chunk.cxx:25:
./Chunk.cxx:26:    for (int z = 0; z < 256; z++)

./Chunk.cxx:28:        for (int x = 0; x < 16; x++)

./Chunk.cxx:30:            for (int y = 0; y < 16; y++)
./Chunk.cxx:31:            {
./Chunk.cxx:32:                const double surfaceNoise = 10.f - floor(perlin.octave2D_01((x + cmx) * .02f, (y + cmy) * .02f, 2) * 10);
./Chunk.cxx:33:                const double stoneNoise = 8.f - floor(perlin.octave2D_01((x + cmx) * .025f, (y + cmy) * .025f, 6) * 8);
./Chunk.cxx:34:                int blockType;
./Chunk.cxx:35:
./Chunk.cxx:36:                int zP = z + surfaceNoise;
./Chunk.cxx:37:                int height = 60 + (int)surfaceNoise; // grass/dirt surface
./Chunk.cxx:38:                int stoneHeight = 50 + (int)stoneNoise;
./Chunk.cxx:39:
./Chunk.cxx:40:                if (z > height)
./Chunk.cxx:41:                    blockType = AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:42:                else if (z == height)
./Chunk.cxx:43:                    blockType = GRASS;
./Chunk.cxx:44:                else if (z > stoneHeight)
./Chunk.cxx:45:                    blockType = DIRT;
./Chunk.cxx:46:                else if (z == 0)
./Chunk.cxx:47:                    blockType = BEDROCK;
./Chunk.cxx:48:                else

./Chunk.cxx:51:                voxels.back().setType(BlockType(blockType));
./Chunk.cxx:52:
./Chunk.cxx:53:                // storing global coords for GC detection
./Chunk.cxx:54:                voxels.back().setPosition({x + 0.5f + cmx,
./Chunk.cxx:55:                                           y + 0.5f + cmy,
./Chunk.cxx:56:                                           z + 0.5f});

./PerlinNoise.hpp:254:		SIVPERLIN_CONCEPT_URBG
./PerlinNoise.hpp:255:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:256:		inline std::uint64_t Random(const std::uint64_t max, URBG&& urbg)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:257:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:258:			return (urbg() % (max + 1));
./PerlinNoise.hpp:259:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:260:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:261:		template <class RandomIt, class URBG>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:262:		inline void Shuffle(RandomIt first, RandomIt last, URBG&& urbg)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:263:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:264:			if (first == last)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:265:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:266:				return;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:267:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:268:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:269:			using difference_type = typename std::iterator_traits<RandomIt>::difference_type;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:270:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:271:			for (RandomIt it = first + 1; it < last; ++it)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:272:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:273:				const std::uint64_t n = static_cast<std::uint64_t>(it - first);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:274:				std::iter_swap(it, first + static_cast<difference_type>(Random(n, std::forward<URBG>(urbg))));
./PerlinNoise.hpp:275:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:276:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:277:		//

./PerlinNoise.hpp:282:		inline constexpr Float Fade(const Float t) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:283:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:284:			return t * t * t * (t * (t * 6 - 15) + 10);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:285:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:286:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:287:		template <class Float>

./PerlinNoise.hpp:290:		{

./PerlinNoise.hpp:296:		inline constexpr Float Grad(const std::uint8_t hash, const Float x, const Float y, const Float z) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:297:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:298:			const std::uint8_t h = hash & 15;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:299:			const Float u = h < 8 ? x : y;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:300:			const Float v = h < 4 ? y : h == 12 || h == 14 ? x : z;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:301:			return ((h & 1) == 0 ? u : -u) + ((h & 2) == 0 ? v : -v);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:302:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:303:

./PerlinNoise.hpp:490:	inline typename BasicPerlinNoise<Float>::value_type BasicPerlinNoise<Float>::noise3D(const value_type x, const value_type y, const value_type z) const noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:491:	{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:492:		const value_type _x = std::floor(x);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:493:		const value_type _y = std::floor(y);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:494:		const value_type _z = std::floor(z);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:495:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:496:		const std::int32_t ix = static_cast<std::int32_t>(_x) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:497:		const std::int32_t iy = static_cast<std::int32_t>(_y) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:498:		const std::int32_t iz = static_cast<std::int32_t>(_z) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:499:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:500:		const value_type fx = (x - _x);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:501:		const value_type fy = (y - _y);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:502:		const value_type fz = (z - _z);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:503:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:504:		const value_type u = perlin_detail::Fade(fx);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:505:		const value_type v = perlin_detail::Fade(fy);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:506:		const value_type w = perlin_detail::Fade(fz);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:507:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:508:		const std::uint8_t A = (m_permutation[ix & 255] + iy) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:509:		const std::uint8_t B = (m_permutation[(ix + 1) & 255] + iy) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:510:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:511:		const std::uint8_t AA = (m_permutation[A] + iz) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:512:		const std::uint8_t AB = (m_permutation[(A + 1) & 255] + iz) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:513:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:514:		const std::uint8_t BA = (m_permutation[B] + iz) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:515:		const std::uint8_t BB = (m_permutation[(B + 1) & 255] + iz) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:516:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:517:		const value_type p0 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[AA], fx, fy, fz);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:518:		const value_type p1 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[BA], fx - 1, fy, fz);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:519:		const value_type p2 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[AB], fx, fy - 1, fz);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:520:		const value_type p3 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[BB], fx - 1, fy - 1, fz);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:521:		const value_type p4 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[(AA + 1) & 255], fx, fy, fz - 1);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:522:		const value_type p5 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[(BA + 1) & 255], fx - 1, fy, fz - 1);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:523:		const value_type p6 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[(AB + 1) & 255], fx, fy - 1, fz - 1);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:524:		const value_type p7 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[(BB + 1) & 255], fx - 1, fy - 1, fz - 1);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:525:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:526:		const value_type q0 = perlin_detail::Lerp(p0, p1, u);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:527:		const value_type q1 = perlin_detail::Lerp(p2, p3, u);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:528:		const value_type q2 = perlin_detail::Lerp(p4, p5, u);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:529:		const value_type q3 = perlin_detail::Lerp(p6, p7, u);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:530:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:531:		const value_type r0 = perlin_detail::Lerp(q0, q1, v);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:532:		const value_type r1 = perlin_detail::Lerp(q2, q3, v);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:533:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:534:		return perlin_detail::Lerp(r0, r1, w);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:535:	}

./Player.cxx:13:void Player::resolveAxis(float amount, int axis, float &vertVel)
./Player.cxx:14:{
./Player.cxx:15:    auto rebuildAABB = [&]()
./Player.cxx:16:    {
./Player.cxx:17:        aabb.max = camera->cameraPos + glm::vec3(0.2f, 0.2f, 0.0f);
./Player.cxx:18:        aabb.min = camera->cameraPos - glm::vec3(0.2f, 0.2f, 1.8f);
./Player.cxx:19:    };
./Player.cxx:20:
./Player.cxx:21:    if (axis == 0)
./Player.cxx:22:        camera->cameraPos.x += amount;
./Player.cxx:23:    else if (axis == 1)
./Player.cxx:24:        camera->cameraPos.y += amount;
./Player.cxx:25:    else
./Player.cxx:26:        camera->cameraPos.z += amount;
./Player.cxx:27:
./Player.cxx:28:    rebuildAABB();
./Player.cxx:29:
./Player.cxx:30:    int minX = (int)floor(aabb.min.x), maxX = (int)floor(aabb.max.x);
./Player.cxx:31:    int minY = (int)floor(aabb.min.y), maxY = (int)floor(aabb.max.y);
./Player.cxx:32:    int minZ = (int)floor(aabb.min.z), maxZ = (int)floor(aabb.max.z);
./Player.cxx:33:
./Player.cxx:34:    for (int x = minX; x <= maxX; ++x)
./Player.cxx:35:        for (int y = minY; y <= maxY; ++y)
./Player.cxx:36:            for (int z = minZ; z <= maxZ; ++z)
./Player.cxx:37:            {
./Player.cxx:38:                Voxel *voxel = gameObjectPool.getVoxelGlobal({x, y, z});
./Player.cxx:39:                if (!voxel || voxel->getBlockType() == AIR)
./Player.cxx:40:                    continue;
./Player.cxx:41:                if (!checkAABBOverlap(aabb, voxel->aabb))
./Player.cxx:42:                    continue;
./Player.cxx:43:
./Player.cxx:44:                // Calculate penetration depth on this axis
./Player.cxx:45:                // If it's far larger than this frame's movement, player is deeply
./Player.cxx:46:                // embedded — skip to avoid flinging them out
./Player.cxx:47:                float penetration = 0.0f;
./Player.cxx:48:                if (axis == 0)
./Player.cxx:49:                    penetration = (amount > 0) ? (aabb.max.x - voxel->aabb.min.x) : (voxel->aabb.max.x - aabb.min.x);
./Player.cxx:50:                if (axis == 1)
./Player.cxx:51:                    penetration = (amount > 0) ? (aabb.max.y - voxel->aabb.min.y) : (voxel->aabb.max.y - aabb.min.y);
./Player.cxx:52:                if (axis == 2)
./Player.cxx:53:                    penetration = (amount > 0) ? (aabb.max.z - voxel->aabb.min.z) : (voxel->aabb.max.z - aabb.min.z);
./Player.cxx:54:
./Player.cxx:55:                if (penetration > fabs(amount) + 0.5f)
./Player.cxx:56:                    continue; // deeply embedded, skip
./Player.cxx:57:
./Player.cxx:58:                switch (axis)
./Player.cxx:59:                {
./Player.cxx:60:                case 0:
./Player.cxx:61:                    camera->cameraPos.x = (amount > 0)
./Player.cxx:62:                                              ? voxel->aabb.min.x - 0.2f
./Player.cxx:63:                                              : voxel->aabb.max.x + 0.2f;
./Player.cxx:64:                    break;
./Player.cxx:65:
./Player.cxx:66:                case 1:
./Player.cxx:67:                    camera->cameraPos.y = (amount > 0)
./Player.cxx:68:                                              ? voxel->aabb.min.y - 0.2f
./Player.cxx:69:                                              : voxel->aabb.max.y + 0.2f;
./Player.cxx:70:                    break;
./Player.cxx:71:
./Player.cxx:72:                case 2:
./Player.cxx:73:                    if (amount < 0)
./Player.cxx:74:                    {
./Player.cxx:75:                        camera->cameraPos.z = voxel->aabb.max.z + 1.8f;
./Player.cxx:76:                        vertVel = 0.0f;
./Player.cxx:77:                        playerState.onGround = true;
./Player.cxx:78:                    }
./Player.cxx:79:                    else
./Player.cxx:80:                    {
./Player.cxx:81:                        camera->cameraPos.z = voxel->aabb.min.z - 0.01f;
./Player.cxx:82:                        vertVel = 0.0f;
./Player.cxx:83:                    }
./Player.cxx:84:                    break;
./Player.cxx:85:                }
./Player.cxx:86:
./Player.cxx:87:                rebuildAABB();
./Player.cxx:88:            }
./Player.cxx:89:}

./Player.cxx:115:void Player::handlePlayerMovement(UniformBufferObject &UBO,
./Player.cxx:116:                                  VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent,
./Player.cxx:117:                                  Event &event)
./Player.cxx:118:{
./Player.cxx:119:    constexpr float GRAVITY = 0.00025f; // tune
./Player.cxx:120:    constexpr float JUMP_FORCE = 0.10f; // tune
./Player.cxx:121:    constexpr float TERMINAL_VEL = -.30f;
./Player.cxx:122:
./Player.cxx:123:    static float vertVel = 0.0f;
./Player.cxx:124:
./Player.cxx:125:    camera->updateUBO(UBO, swapChainExtent, event);
./Player.cxx:126:
./Player.cxx:127:    glm::vec3 delta(0.0f);
./Player.cxx:128:
./Player.cxx:129:    if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_W))
./Player.cxx:130:        delta += camera->forwardFlat * camera->speed;
./Player.cxx:131:    if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_S))
./Player.cxx:132:        delta -= camera->forwardFlat * camera->speed;
./Player.cxx:133:    if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_A))
./Player.cxx:134:        delta += camera->right * camera->speed;
./Player.cxx:135:    if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_D))
./Player.cxx:136:        delta -= camera->right * camera->speed;
./Player.cxx:137:
./Player.cxx:138:    if (playerState.onGround && event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_SPACE))
./Player.cxx:139:        vertVel = JUMP_FORCE;
./Player.cxx:140:    if (!playerState.onGround)
./Player.cxx:141:        vertVel -= GRAVITY * float(event.dt);
./Player.cxx:142:    if (vertVel < TERMINAL_VEL)
./Player.cxx:143:        vertVel = TERMINAL_VEL;
./Player.cxx:144:
./Player.cxx:145:    delta.z += vertVel;
./Player.cxx:146:    if (std::abs(vertVel) < 0.00001f)
./Player.cxx:147:        vertVel = 0.0f;
./Player.cxx:148:
./Player.cxx:149:    resolveAxis(delta.x, 0, vertVel);
./Player.cxx:150:    resolveAxis(delta.y, 1, vertVel);
./Player.cxx:151:    playerState.onGround = false;
./Player.cxx:152:    resolveAxis(delta.z, 2, vertVel);
./Player.cxx:153:}

./Textures.cxx:234:void u_Texture::transitionImageLayout(VkImage image, VkFormat format, VkImageLayout oldLayout, VkImageLayout newLayout, uint32_t mipLevels)
./Textures.cxx:235:{
./Textures.cxx:236:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./Textures.cxx:237:
./Textures.cxx:238:    VkImageMemoryBarrier barrier{};
./Textures.cxx:239:    barrier.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_IMAGE_MEMORY_BARRIER;
./Textures.cxx:240:    barrier.oldLayout = oldLayout;
./Textures.cxx:241:    barrier.newLayout = newLayout;
./Textures.cxx:242:
./Textures.cxx:243:    // We are not transfering queue family ownership rn!!!
./Textures.cxx:244:    barrier.srcQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:245:    barrier.dstQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:246:
./Textures.cxx:247:    barrier.image = image;
./Textures.cxx:248:    barrier.subresourceRange.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;

./Textures.cxx:250:    barrier.subresourceRange.levelCount = mipLevels;

./Textures.cxx:252:    barrier.subresourceRange.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:253:
./Textures.cxx:254:    barrier.srcAccessMask = 0; // todo
./Textures.cxx:255:    barrier.dstAccessMask = 0; // todo
./Textures.cxx:256:

./Textures.cxx:258:    VkPipelineStageFlags destinationStage;
./Textures.cxx:259:
./Textures.cxx:260:    if (oldLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED && newLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL)

./Textures.cxx:262:        barrier.srcAccessMask = 0;
./Textures.cxx:263:        barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:264:

./Textures.cxx:267:    }
./Textures.cxx:268:    else if (oldLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL && newLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_SHADER_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL)
./Textures.cxx:269:    {
./Textures.cxx:270:        barrier.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:271:        barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_SHADER_READ_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:272:
./Textures.cxx:273:        sourceStage = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:274:        destinationStage = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_FRAGMENT_SHADER_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:275:    }
./Textures.cxx:276:    else
./Textures.cxx:277:    {
./Textures.cxx:278:        throw std::invalid_argument("unsupported layout transition!");
./Textures.cxx:279:    }
./Textures.cxx:280:
./Textures.cxx:281:    vkCmdPipelineBarrier(

./Textures.cxx:283:        sourceStage, destinationStage,
./Textures.cxx:284:        0,
./Textures.cxx:285:        0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:286:        0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:287:        1, &barrier);

./Textures.cxx:314:void u_Texture::generateMipmaps(VkImage image, VkFormat imageFormat, int32_t texWidth, int32_t texHeight, uint32_t mipLevels)
./Textures.cxx:315:{
./Textures.cxx:316:    // Check if image format supports linear blitting
./Textures.cxx:317:    VkFormatProperties formatProperties;
./Textures.cxx:318:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceFormatProperties(physicalDevice, imageFormat, &formatProperties);
./Textures.cxx:319:
./Textures.cxx:320:    if (!(formatProperties.optimalTilingFeatures & VK_FORMAT_FEATURE_SAMPLED_IMAGE_FILTER_LINEAR_BIT))
./Textures.cxx:321:    {
./Textures.cxx:322:        throw std::runtime_error("texture image format does not support linear blitting!");
./Textures.cxx:323:    }
./Textures.cxx:324:
./Textures.cxx:325:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./Textures.cxx:326:
./Textures.cxx:327:    VkImageMemoryBarrier barrier{};
./Textures.cxx:328:    barrier.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_IMAGE_MEMORY_BARRIER;
./Textures.cxx:329:    barrier.image = image;
./Textures.cxx:330:    barrier.srcQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:331:    barrier.dstQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:332:    barrier.subresourceRange.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:333:    barrier.subresourceRange.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:334:    barrier.subresourceRange.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:335:    barrier.subresourceRange.levelCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:336:

./Textures.cxx:338:    int32_t mipHeight = texHeight;
./Textures.cxx:339:
./Textures.cxx:340:    for (uint32_t i = 1; i < mipLevels; i++)

./Textures.cxx:345:        barrier.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:346:        barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_READ_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:347:
./Textures.cxx:348:        vkCmdPipelineBarrier(commandBuffer,
./Textures.cxx:349:                             VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT, VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT, 0,
./Textures.cxx:350:                             0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:351:                             0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:352:                             1, &barrier);
./Textures.cxx:353:
./Textures.cxx:354:        VkImageBlit blit{};
./Textures.cxx:355:        blit.srcOffsets[0] = {0, 0, 0};

./Textures.cxx:357:        blit.srcSubresource.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:358:        blit.srcSubresource.mipLevel = i - 1;

./Textures.cxx:360:        blit.srcSubresource.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:361:        blit.dstOffsets[0] = {0, 0, 0};

./Textures.cxx:363:        blit.dstSubresource.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;

./Textures.cxx:369:                       image, VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_SRC_OPTIMAL,
./Textures.cxx:370:                       image, VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL,

./Textures.cxx:373:
./Textures.cxx:374:        barrier.oldLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_SRC_OPTIMAL;

./Textures.cxx:379:        vkCmdPipelineBarrier(commandBuffer,
./Textures.cxx:380:                             VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT, VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_FRAGMENT_SHADER_BIT, 0,

./Textures.cxx:382:                             0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:383:                             1, &barrier);
./Textures.cxx:384:

./Textures.cxx:386:            mipWidth /= 2;
./Textures.cxx:387:        if (mipHeight > 1)
./Textures.cxx:388:            mipHeight /= 2;
./Textures.cxx:389:    }
./Textures.cxx:390:

./Textures.cxx:392:    barrier.oldLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:393:    barrier.newLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_SHADER_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL;

./intiVk.cxx:317:int HelloTriangleApplication::rateDeviceSuitablity(VkPhysicalDevice device)
./intiVk.cxx:318:{
./intiVk.cxx:319:    VkPhysicalDeviceProperties props;
./intiVk.cxx:320:    VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures feats;
./intiVk.cxx:321:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceProperties(device, &props);
./intiVk.cxx:322:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceFeatures(device, &feats);
./intiVk.cxx:323:
./intiVk.cxx:324:    int score = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:325:
./intiVk.cxx:326:    std::cout << "Device: " << props.deviceName << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:327:
./intiVk.cxx:328:    // Prefer discrete or integrated GPU
./intiVk.cxx:329:    if (props.deviceType == VK_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_TYPE_DISCRETE_GPU)
./intiVk.cxx:330:        score += 10000;
./intiVk.cxx:331:    else if (props.deviceType == VK_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_TYPE_INTEGRATED_GPU)
./intiVk.cxx:332:        score += 5000;
./intiVk.cxx:333:
./intiVk.cxx:334:    // Bigger textures = better
./intiVk.cxx:335:    score += props.limits.maxImageDimension2D;
./intiVk.cxx:336:
./intiVk.cxx:337:    // Useful features
./intiVk.cxx:338:    if (feats.samplerAnisotropy)
./intiVk.cxx:339:        score += 1000;
./intiVk.cxx:340:    if (feats.shaderInt64)
./intiVk.cxx:341:        score += 500;
./intiVk.cxx:342:    if (feats.wideLines)
./intiVk.cxx:343:        score += 300;
./intiVk.cxx:344:
./intiVk.cxx:345:#ifdef __APPLE__
./intiVk.cxx:346:    // Metal backend doesn’t support geometry/tessellation shaders
./intiVk.cxx:347:    score += 1500;
./intiVk.cxx:348:#else
./intiVk.cxx:349:    if (!feats.geometryShader)
./intiVk.cxx:350:        return 0; // skip if no geometry shader
./intiVk.cxx:351:#endif
./intiVk.cxx:352:
./intiVk.cxx:353:    return score;
./intiVk.cxx:354:}

./intiVk.cxx:584:// Extent defines the resolution of the image
./intiVk.cxx:585:// MacOS has a fixed extent while other windowing systems have a varible extent which is clamped to the window bounds
./intiVk.cxx:586:// also High-DPI displays like Apple Liquid Retina displays have to be configure in a sepreate way
./intiVk.cxx:587:VkExtent2D HelloTriangleApplication::chooseSwapExtent(const VkSurfaceCapabilitiesKHR &capabilities)
./intiVk.cxx:588:{
./intiVk.cxx:589:#ifdef __APPLE__
./intiVk.cxx:590:    // MoltenVK on macOS (Retina-safe)
./intiVk.cxx:591:    int width, height;
./intiVk.cxx:592:    glfwGetFramebufferSize(_window, &width, &height);
./intiVk.cxx:593:
./intiVk.cxx:594:    VkExtent2D actualExtent = {
./intiVk.cxx:595:        static_cast<uint32_t>(width),
./intiVk.cxx:596:        static_cast<uint32_t>(height)};
./intiVk.cxx:597:
./intiVk.cxx:598:    return actualExtent; // Always use framebuffer size on Retina
./intiVk.cxx:599:#else
./intiVk.cxx:600:    // Metal IE: the size is predifined and is not UINT 32 max. therefore, use the size provided by the system
./intiVk.cxx:601:    if (capabilities.currentExtent.width != std::numeric_limits<uint32_t>::max())
./intiVk.cxx:602:    {
./intiVk.cxx:603:        return capabilities.currentExtent;
./intiVk.cxx:604:    }
./intiVk.cxx:605:    // The surface does not have a fixed size and you must create it by yourself
./intiVk.cxx:606:    else
./intiVk.cxx:607:    {
./intiVk.cxx:608:        int width, height;
./intiVk.cxx:609:        glfwGetFramebufferSize(_window, &width, &height);
./intiVk.cxx:610:
./intiVk.cxx:611:        VkExtent2D actualExtent =
./intiVk.cxx:612:            {
./intiVk.cxx:613:                static_cast<uint32_t>(width),
./intiVk.cxx:614:                static_cast<uint32_t>(height)};
./intiVk.cxx:615:
./intiVk.cxx:616:        actualExtent.width = std::clamp(actualExtent.width, capabilities.minImageExtent.width, capabilities.maxImageExtent.width);
./intiVk.cxx:617:
./intiVk.cxx:618:        actualExtent.height = std::clamp(actualExtent.height, capabilities.minImageExtent.height, capabilities.maxImageExtent.height);
./intiVk.cxx:619:
./intiVk.cxx:620:        return actualExtent;
./intiVk.cxx:621:    }
./intiVk.cxx:622:
./intiVk.cxx:623:#endif
./intiVk.cxx:624:}

./intiVk.cxx:627:void HelloTriangleApplication::createVertexBuffer()
./intiVk.cxx:628:{

./intiVk.cxx:635:    // TX
./intiVk.cxx:636:    createBuffer(bufferSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT, VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_VISIBLE_BIT | VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_CACHED_BIT, stagingBuffer, stagingBufferMemory);

./intiVk.cxx:643:

./intiVk.cxx:645:    // TX

./intiVk.cxx:648:    // but we still have to copy the memory contents manully

./intiVk.cxx:650:
./intiVk.cxx:651:    vkDestroyBuffer(device, stagingBuffer, nullptr);

./utils.cxx:92:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to submit copy command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:93:    }

./utils.cxx:95:
